posted:Posted December 22, 2023
msg:I booked a 1.7k room with a view of the pine trees, because there was no table or chair in the room with a view. There was only one chair outside. I changed to a room with a real view of the pine trees, but I couldn't see the view. I changed rooms just to have a place to sit in the room. The room as a whole is just a bed room, the lighting is dim, the refrigerator is empty, the bathroom is large and the configuration is very high. The Dyson hair dryer is easy to use, but the water pressure is not high and the hot water is unstable. The rest is roughly the same as a four-star hotel.
The public area has everything that should be normal, but the maintenance is not timely, the cigarette butts on the table, the socks on the tatami, and the check-in balcony are placed in a mess, and management needs to be strengthened.
The guest room door has no safety lock, there is no floor function area sign in the corridor, and the fire extinguisher is placed directly in the corridor (there is a huge safety hazard, the fire should not have routine inspections, and the market supervision and management bureau can directly suspend business for rectification)
The hot spring pool is a gimmick to attract bookings. The free public pool can only be used from 3 to 6 pm, and reservations must be made in advance because there is only one public pool and it is not large. **The promotion of bathing in the evening is actually the night view of the public pool (but it is not open at night. I just wanted to take my children to bathe in the evening after playing during the day). I felt like I was being tricked.
Reminder: The hotel can pick up and drop off when going out. On the first day we went out, we asked the housekeeper how to go out, and we were told to take a taxi. As a result, we couldn't get a taxi and walked back and forth. Later, the aunt in the restaurant told us that we could ask the driver to pick us up (speechless ğŸ˜¶), and then we called the front desk to arrange the vehicle in and out. All the drivers are very good.
In addition, there is no medical emergency plan. It is difficult to buy medicine late at night. The hotel only provides external medicine. Be sure to prepare oral medicine in case of diarrhea caused by unclean food at tourist attractions at night.
In short, the 1.7k room price is very controversial. Heavy snow is a factor in price increases, but the overall room price in Lushan is not high. There is a Zhihong Hotel nearby for comparison.

msg:The two days staying in Songmo was also the highlight of the trip to Mount Lu. It is very suitable for friends who plan to have a slow leisure time.

All the staff were very enthusiastic and patient. The lady at the front desk reminded me of the route up the mountain two days before the trip; the driver took us to the Lushan Cableway and the main street; the hotel boy helped us carry our suitcases and brought refreshments upstairs. (Working days in the off-season are not too busy, so you may have more time to take care of our needs.)

Very clean, beautiful environment and first-class facilities. Compared with other Lushan B&Bs, it is basically impeccable. The hotel is very new and there are no old or damaged facilities. Generally speaking, the more expensive the room, the larger the area inside the suite. After all, in the mountains, you wouldnâ€™t expect the size of a presidential suite.

Breakfast, lunch and afternoon tea are all very exquisite and delicious. The fruit baskets given away every day are fresh. The room is equipped with Evian mineral water, mountain spring water and carbonated drinks for free. There is free tea in the public areas on each floor. The coffee bean grinding espresso next to the restaurant on the first floor is very good.

I feel that the public area covers at least 30% of the total area, including restaurants, gyms, tea rooms, terraces, observation decks, gardens, etc. Different from the concept of selling rooms in ordinary hotels or B&Bs, Songmo is more suitable for leisure.

The hotel should continue to do a good job in maintaining the facilities and hope to have the same good experience next time.

(In addition, everyoneâ€™s experience in the same hotel is different, which is closely related to their expectations, purpose, visit time, mentality and travel experience. It is recommended that friends do not stay in the hotel with the mentality that they should have a golden luxury experience after spending a little money.)

Let me share some practical information with you:
1. The hotel will pick up guests at the Lushan Cableway Station. There will be no pick-up or drop-off at the airport, train station or down the mountain.
2. The hotel can be reached on foot from Meilu. If you go to other attractions, it is very convenient to take a sightseeing bus.
3. Breakfast, lunch, dinner and refreshments are available at the hotel. The price is more expensive than outside restaurants, depending on whether you want to save money or trouble. (Whether the room price includes breakfast should be selected when booking)
